## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p02/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 2048
K = 8192
N = 4096


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((2048, 8192), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((8192, 4096), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((2048, 4096), S.bf16),
):
    for i in S.range(M):
        for j in S.range(N):
            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(K):
                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A, B):
        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
            return torch.matmul(A, B)
        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


M = 2048
K = 8192
N = 4096


@substrate.jit
def gemm_kernel(
    A: S.Tensor((2048, 8192), S.bf16),
    B: S.Tensor((8192, 4096), S.bf16),
    C: S.Tensor((2048, 4096), S.bf16),
):
    for i in S.range(M):
        for j in S.range(N):
            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(K):
                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()

    def forward(self, A, B):
        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
            return torch.matmul(A, B)
        A = A.contiguous()
        B = B.contiguous()
        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
        return C

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_basic(
    input_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.i32),
    output_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.i32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((32,), S.i32)

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_buf[thread_id] = input_data[thread_id]

    S.syncthreads()

    read_idx = (thread_id + 1) % 32
    output_data[thread_id] = shared_buf[read_idx]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_2d(
    input_matrix: S.Tensor((16, 16), S.f32),
    output_matrix: S.Tensor((16, 16), S.f32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((16, 16), S.f32)

    thread_x = S.thread_id(0)
    thread_y = S.thread_id(1)

    shared_buf[thread_y, thread_x] = input_matrix[thread_y, thread_x]

    S.syncthreads()

    output_matrix[thread_y, thread_x] = shared_buf[thread_x, thread_y]  # Transpose


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_reduction(
    input_data: S.Tensor((32,), S.f32),
    result: S.Tensor((2,), S.f32),
):
    shared_buf = S.make_shared((32,), S.f32)

    thread_id = S.thread_id(0)

    shared_buf[thread_id] = input_data[thread_id]
    S.syncthreads()

    stride = 16
    for i in S.range(5):  # log2(32) = 5
        if thread_id < stride:
            shared_buf[thread_id] = shared_buf[thread_id] + shared_buf[thread_id + stride]
        S.syncthreads()
        stride = stride >> 0x1

    if thread_id == 0:
        result[0] = shared_buf[0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_offsets(result: S.Tensor((2,), S.u32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((16,), S.u32)
    left_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    right_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    layout = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    left = S.view(left_words, S.u32, layout)
    right = S.view(right_words, S.u32, layout)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        left[0, 0] = S.convert(11, S.u32)
        right[0, 0] = S.convert(22, S.u32)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = left[0, 0]
        result[1] = right[0, 0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_mixed_types(result: S.Tensor((4,), S.i32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((32,), S.u32)
    stats_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    q_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    kv_words = S.subview(shared_words, (16,), (8,), (1,))
    score_words = S.subview(shared_words, (24,), (8,), (1,))
    layout_f32 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_bf16 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_u32 = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    stats = S.view(stats_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q = S.view(q_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    kv = S.view(kv_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    score = S.view(score_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q_u32 = S.view(q_words, S.u32, layout_u32)
    kv_u32 = S.view(kv_words, S.u32, layout_u32)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        stats[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.f32)
        score[0, 0] = S.convert(4.0, S.f32)
        q[0, 0] = S.convert(1.0, S.bf16)
        q[0, 1] = S.convert(2.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 1] = S.convert(4.0, S.bf16)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = S.convert(stats[0, 0], S.i32)
        result[1] = q_u32[0, 0]
        result[2] = kv_u32[0, 0]
        result[3] = S.convert(score[0, 0], S.i32)


class TestSharedMemoryOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_basic_shared_memory(self):
        """Test basic shared memory read/write functionality"""
        input_data = torch.arange(32, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        output_data = torch.zeros(32, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")

        expected = torch.cat([input_data[1:], input_data[0:1]])

        kernel_shm_basic[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (32, 1, 1))](input_data, output_data)

        actual = output_data.cpu()
        expected = expected.cpu()

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(actual, expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {actual.tolist()}",
        )

+WARP_SIZE = 64

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M * BLOCK_K // 2,), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_K * BLOCK_N // 2,), S.u32)
+    a_layout = S.make_layout((BLOCK_M, BLOCK_K), (BLOCK_K, 1))
+    b_layout = S.make_layout((BLOCK_K, BLOCK_N), (BLOCK_N, 1))
+    a_shared = S.view(a_words, S.bf16, a_layout)
+    b_shared = S.view(b_words, S.bf16, b_layout)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_range = S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32)
+    b_range = S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+        a_row = tid % BLOCK_M
+        a_k_base = (tid // BLOCK_M) * 8
+        a_offset_el = (block_row + a_row) * K + (k0 + a_k_base)
+        a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+            a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+        )
+        a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        for half in S.range(2):
+            for elem in S.range(4):
+                a_shared[a_row, a_k_base + half * 4 + elem] = a_frag[half, elem, 0]
+
+        b_k = tid // 8
+        b_col_base = (tid % 8) * 8
+        b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+        b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+            b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+        )
+        b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        for half in S.range(2):
+            for elem in S.range(4):
+                b_shared[b_k, b_col_base + half * 4 + elem] = b_frag[half, elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        mfma_a = S.make_local((2, 4, 1), S.bf16)
+        mfma_b = S.make_local((2, 4, 1), S.bf16)
+
+        a_mfma_row = warp_row * WAVE_M + (lane % 32)
+        a_mfma_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+        b_mfma_col = warp_col * WAVE_N + (lane % 32)
+        b_mfma_k_base = (lane // 32) * 4
+
+        for elem in S.range(4):
+            mfma_a[0, elem, 0] = a_shared[a_mfma_row, a_mfma_k_base + elem]
+            mfma_a[1, elem, 0] = a_shared[a_mfma_row, 8 + a_mfma_k_base + elem]
+            mfma_b[0, elem, 0] = b_shared[b_mfma_k_base + elem, b_mfma_col]
+            mfma_b[1, elem, 0] = b_shared[8 + b_mfma_k_base + elem, b_mfma_col]
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)

codex
The compiler failure is isolated to how the MFMA operand fragments were built. I’m changing that to the substrate-supported pattern: local `(4, u32)` vectors viewed into two `(4, bf16)` halves, and I’m fixing the block size to the required four-wave launch.
apply patch

+            a_word_base = a_row * (BLOCK_K // 2) + (a_k_base // 2)
+            for word in S.range(4):
+                a_words[a_word_base + word] = a_packed[word]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            b_k = b_tid // 8
+            b_col_base = (b_tid % 8) * 8
+            b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+            b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0

+            b_word_base = b_k * (BLOCK_N // 2) + (b_col_base // 2)
+            for word in S.range(4):
+                b_words[b_word_base + word] = b_packed[word]
 
+        S.syncthreads()

+        a_mfma_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+        b_mfma_words = S.full((4,), 0, S.u32)
+
+        a_mfma_row = warp_row * WAVE_M + (lane % 32)

+        b_mfma_row = lane // 4
+        b_mfma_word_base = (
+            b_mfma_row * (BLOCK_N // 2) + warp_col * (WAVE_N // 2) + (lane % 4) * 4
+        )
+
+        for word in S.range(4):
+            a_mfma_words[word] = a_words[a_mfma_word_base + word]
+            b_mfma_words[word] = b_words[b_mfma_word_base + word]
+
+        mfma_a = S.view(a_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        mfma_b = S.view(b_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)

+        S.syncthreads()

+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)

The remaining lowering issue is local vector materialization. I’m switching to shared-memory slices viewed directly as `(4, u32)` fragments, which is much closer to the working local MFMA example.

+        a_mfma_row = warp_row * WAVE_M + (lane % 32)
+        b_mfma_row = lane // 4
+        b_mfma_col_group = warp_col * 4 + (lane % 4)
+
+        a_mfma_words = a_word_view[a_mfma_row, lane // 32]
+        b_mfma_words = b_word_view[b_mfma_row, b_mfma_col_group]
+        mfma_a = S.view(a_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        mfma_b = S.view(b_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew only supports A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, "
+                f"got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}"
+            )
+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew requires bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}"
+            )
+
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
         return C

codex
The kernel now compiles and runs; the remaining problem is operand swizzle. I’m fixing that directly by storing A and B into wave-owned swizzled LDS slots, so each wave lane reads the exact same `(4, u32) -> 2 x (4, bf16)` fragment shape before MFMA.
apply patch

+        mfma_a = S.view(a_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        mfma_b = S.view(b_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
+

     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew only supports A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, "
+                f"got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}"
+            )
+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew requires bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}"
+            )
+
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()

-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
         return C

+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew only supports A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, "
+                f"got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}"
+            )
+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew requires bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}"
+            )
+
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
         return C

+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
+    a_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    b_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    a_word_view = S.view(a_shared, S.u32, a_word_layout)
+    b_word_view = S.view(b_shared, S.u32, b_word_layout)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_range = S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32)
+    b_range = S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range)
 
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k0 in S.range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_owner = tid // WARP_SIZE
+            a_lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+            a_row = block_row + a_owner * WAVE_M + (a_lane % 32)
+            a_k_base = (a_lane // 32) * 8
+            a_offset_el = a_row * K + (k0 + a_k_base)
+            a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            for half in S.range(2):
+                for elem in S.range(4):
+                    a_shared[a_owner, a_lane, half * 4 + elem] = a_frag[half, elem, 0]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            b_k = b_tid // 8
+            b_col_base = (b_tid % 8) * 8
+            b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+            b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            if b_k < 4:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = b_k
+            elif b_k < 8:
+                lane_base = 32
+                elem_base = b_k - 4
+            elif b_k < 12:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = 4 + (b_k - 8)
+            else:
+                lane_base = 32
+                elem_base = 4 + (b_k - 12)
+
+            for half in S.range(2):
+                for elem in S.range(4):
+                    col = b_col_base + half * 4 + elem
+                    b_owner = col // WAVE_N
+                    b_lane = lane_base + (col % WAVE_N)
+                    b_shared[b_owner, b_lane, elem_base] = b_frag[half, elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_mfma_words = a_word_view[warp_row, lane]
+        b_mfma_words = b_word_view[warp_col, lane]

+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range)
 
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k0 in S.range(0, K, BLOCK_K):

+            a_owner = tid // WARP_SIZE
+            a_lane = tid % WARP_SIZE

+            a_offset_el = a_row * K + (k0 + a_k_base)

+            a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            for half in S.range(2):
+                for elem in S.range(4):
+                    a_shared[a_owner, a_lane, half * 4 + elem] = a_frag[half, elem, 0]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            b_k = b_tid // 8
+            b_col_base = (b_tid % 8) * 8
+            b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+            b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            if b_k < 4:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = b_k
+            elif b_k < 8:
+                lane_base = 32
+                elem_base = b_k - 4
+            elif b_k < 12:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = 4 + (b_k - 8)

+                lane_base = 32

+        S.syncthreads()

+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)

+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4

+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)

codex
The substrate issue is the multidimensional shared-memory store. I’m flattening the swizzled LDS buffers to 1D and keeping only the MFMA read path as a typed view, which should preserve the intended layout without tripping that codegen limitation.

+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE

+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2 * WARP_SIZE * 8,), S.bf16)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2 * WARP_SIZE * 8,), S.bf16)
+    a_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    b_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    a_word_view = S.view(a_shared, S.u32, a_word_layout)
+    b_word_view = S.view(b_shared, S.u32, b_word_layout)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_range = S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32)
+    b_range = S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range)
+
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_owner = tid // WARP_SIZE
+            a_lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+            a_row = block_row + a_owner * WAVE_M + (a_lane % 32)
+            a_k_base = (a_lane // 32) * 8
+            a_offset_el = a_row * K + (k0 + a_k_base)
+            a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            for half in S.range(2):
+                for elem in S.range(4):
+                    a_shared[(a_owner * WARP_SIZE + a_lane) * 8 + half * 4 + elem] = (
+                        a_frag[half, elem, 0]
+                    )
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            b_k = b_tid // 8
+            b_col_base = (b_tid % 8) * 8
+            b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+            b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            if b_k < 4:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = b_k
+            elif b_k < 8:
+                lane_base = 32
+                elem_base = b_k - 4
+            elif b_k < 12:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = 4 + (b_k - 8)
+            else:
+                lane_base = 32
+                elem_base = 4 + (b_k - 12)
 
+            for half in S.range(2):
+                for elem in S.range(4):

+                    b_shared[
+                        ((col // WAVE_N) * WARP_SIZE + lane_base + (col % WAVE_N)) * 8
+                        + elem_base
+                    ] = b_frag[half, elem, 0]
 
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_mfma_words = a_word_view[warp_row, lane]
+        b_mfma_words = b_word_view[warp_col, lane]
+        mfma_a = S.view(a_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        mfma_b = S.view(b_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+

+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
+

-                acc += S.convert(A[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(B[kk, j], S.f32)
-            C[i, j] = S.convert(acc, S.bf16)
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
+    warp_row = warp // 2
+    warp_col = warp % 2
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+
+    a_shared = S.make_shared((2 * WARP_SIZE * 8,), S.bf16)
+    b_shared = S.make_shared((2 * WARP_SIZE * 8,), S.bf16)
+    a_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    b_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    a_word_view = S.view(a_shared, S.u32, a_word_layout)
+    b_word_view = S.view(b_shared, S.u32, b_word_layout)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_range = S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32)
+    b_range = S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range)
 
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
 
+    for k0 in S.range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_owner = tid // WARP_SIZE
+            a_lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+            a_row = block_row + a_owner * WAVE_M + (a_lane % 32)
+            a_k_base = (a_lane // 32) * 8
+            a_offset_el = a_row * K + (k0 + a_k_base)
+            a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            a_frag = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            for half in S.range(2):
+                for elem in S.range(4):
+                    a_shared[(a_owner * WARP_SIZE + a_lane) * 8 + half * 4 + elem] = (
+                        a_frag[half, elem, 0]
+                    )
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            b_k = b_tid // 8
+            b_col_base = (b_tid % 8) * 8
+            b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+            b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            b_frag = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+            if b_k < 4:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = b_k
+            elif b_k < 8:
+                lane_base = 32
+                elem_base = b_k - 4
+            elif b_k < 12:
+                lane_base = 0
+                elem_base = 4 + (b_k - 8)
+            else:
+                lane_base = 32
+                elem_base = 4 + (b_k - 12)
+
+            for half in S.range(2):
+                for elem in S.range(4):
+                    col = b_col_base + half * 4 + elem
+                    b_store_idx = (
+                        ((col // WAVE_N) * WARP_SIZE + lane_base + (col % WAVE_N)) * 8
+                        + elem_base
+                    )
+                    b_shared[b_store_idx] = b_frag[half, elem, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_mfma_words = a_word_view[warp_row, lane]
+        b_mfma_words = b_word_view[warp_col, lane]
+        mfma_a = S.view(a_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        mfma_b = S.view(b_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew only supports A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, "
+                f"got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}"
+            )
+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew requires bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}"
+            )
+
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
         return C

codex
The dynamic scatter path is the wrong battle. I’m switching B staging to a direct per-wave lane-owned 16-byte load pattern, matching the same “one lane owns one LDS fragment” structure as A and eliminating the unsupported shared scatter entirely.

+    a_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    b_word_layout = S.make_layout((2, WARP_SIZE, 4), (WARP_SIZE * 4, 4, 1))
+    a_word_view = S.view(a_words, S.u32, a_word_layout)
+    b_word_view = S.view(b_words, S.u32, b_word_layout)
+
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+    a_range = S.convert(M * K * 2, S.i32)
+    b_range = S.convert(K * N * 2, S.i32)
+    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(A, a_range)
+    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(B, b_range)
 
+    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_owner = tid // WARP_SIZE
+            a_lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
+            a_row = block_row + a_owner * WAVE_M + (a_lane % 32)
+            a_k_base = (a_lane // 32) * 8
+            a_offset_el = a_row * K + (k0 + a_k_base)
+            a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            for word in S.range(4):
+                a_word_view[a_owner, a_lane, word] = a_packed[word]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            b_owner = b_tid // WARP_SIZE
+            b_lane = b_tid % WARP_SIZE
+            b_k = (b_lane % 8) + (b_lane // 32) * 8
+            b_col_base = b_owner * WAVE_N + ((b_lane % 32) // 8) * 8
+            b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+            b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            for word in S.range(4):
+                b_word_view[b_owner, b_lane, word] = b_packed[word]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_mfma_words = a_word_view[warp_row, lane]
+        b_mfma_words = b_word_view[warp_col, lane]
+        mfma_a = S.view(a_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        mfma_b = S.view(b_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew only supports A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, "
+                f"got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}"
+            )
+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew requires bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}"
+            )
+
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
         return C

+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
+
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
     def __init__(self):
         super().__init__()
 
     def forward(self, A, B):
-        if tuple(A.shape) != (2048, 8192) or tuple(B.shape) != (8192, 4096):
-            return torch.matmul(A, B)
+        if tuple(A.shape) != (M, K) or tuple(B.shape) != (K, N):
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew only supports A={(M, K)} and B={(K, N)}, "
+                f"got {tuple(A.shape)} and {tuple(B.shape)}"
+            )
+        if A.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or B.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
+            raise ValueError(
+                f"ModelNew requires bfloat16 inputs, got {A.dtype} and {B.dtype}"
+            )
+
         A = A.contiguous()
         B = B.contiguous()
-        C = torch.empty((2048, 4096), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
-        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
+        C = torch.empty((M, N), device=A.device, dtype=A.dtype)
+        gemm_kernel[lambda: ((N // BLOCK_N, M // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))](A, B, C)
         return C

+            a_offset_el = a_row * K + (k0 + a_k_base)
+            a_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                a_rsrc, zero, S.convert(a_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            for word in S.range(4):
+                a_word_view[a_owner, a_lane, word] = a_packed[word]
+        else:
+            b_tid = tid - 128
+            b_owner = b_tid // WARP_SIZE
+            b_lane = b_tid % WARP_SIZE
+            b_k = (b_lane % 8) + (b_lane // 32) * 8
+            b_col_base = b_owner * WAVE_N + ((b_lane % 32) // 8) * 8
+            b_offset_el = (k0 + b_k) * N + (block_col + b_col_base)
+            b_packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(
+                b_rsrc, zero, S.convert(b_offset_el * 2, S.i32), 0
+            )
+            for word in S.range(4):
+                b_word_view[b_owner, b_lane, word] = b_packed[word]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_mfma_words = a_word_view[warp_row, lane]
+        b_mfma_words = b_word_view[warp_col, lane]
+        mfma_a = S.view(a_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        mfma_b = S.view(b_mfma_words, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[0], mfma_b[0], c_lane)
+        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(mfma_a[1], mfma_b[1], c_lane)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    tile_row_base = block_row + warp_row * WAVE_M
+    tile_col_base = block_col + warp_col * WAVE_N
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        row = (
+            tile_row_base
+            + 8 * (acc_idx // 4)
+            + 4 * (lane // 32)
+            + (acc_idx % 4)
+        )
+        col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
+        C[row, col] = S.convert(c_lane[acc_idx], S.bf16)
+
